### Description

OpenFGA fails to start when configured to use secondary postgres DB and data store metrics enabled.

Steps to reproduce:
1. Enable postgres secondary DB (add `OPENFGA_DATASTORE_SECONDARY_URI` env var)
2. Set `OPENFGA_DATASTORE_METRICS_ENABLED` to `"true"`
3. Start OpenFGA

Observe
```
panic: initialize postgres datastore: configure secondary db: initialize metrics: duplicate metrics collector registration attempted
```


### OpenFGA version

v1.9.2

### How are you running OpenFGA?

In Docker

### What datastore are you using?

Postgres

### OpenFGA Flags

OPENFGA_DATASTORE_METRICS_ENABLED and OPENFGA_METRICS_ENABLED

### Logs

panic: initialize postgres datastore: configure secondary db: initialize metrics: duplicate metrics collector registration attempted

   342	func run(_ *cobra.Command, _ []string) {
   343	        config, err := ReadConfig()
   344	        if err != nil {
   345	                panic(err)
   346	        }
   347	
   348	        if err := config.Verify(); err != nil {
   349	                panic(err)
   350	        }
   351	
   352	        logger := logger.MustNewLogger(config.Log.Format, config.Log.Level, config.Log.TimestampFormat)
   353	        serverCtx := &ServerContext{Logger: logger}
   354	        if err := serverCtx.Run(context.Background(), config); err != nil {
   355	                panic(err)
   356	        }
   357	}

   363	func convertStringArrayToUintArray(stringArray []string) []uint {
   364	        uintArray := []uint{}
   365	        for _, val := range stringArray {
   366	                // note that we have already validated whether the array item is non-negative integer
   367	                valInt, err := strconv.Atoi(val)
   368	                if err == nil {
   369	                        uintArray = append(uintArray, uint(valInt))
   370	                }
   371	        }
   372	        return uintArray
   373	}

   375	// telemetryConfig returns the function that must be called to shut down tracing.
   376	// The context provided to this function should be error-free, or shut down will be incomplete.
   377	func (s *ServerContext) telemetryConfig(config *serverconfig.Config) func() error {
   378	        if config.Trace.Enabled {
   379	                s.Logger.Info(fmt.Sprintf("🕵 tracing enabled: sampling ratio is %v and sending traces to '%s', tls: %t", config.Trace.SampleRatio, config.Trace.OTLP.Endpoint, config.Trace.OTLP.TLS.Enabled))
   380	
   381	                options := []telemetry.TracerOption{
   382	                        telemetry.WithOTLPEndpoint(
   383	                                config.Trace.OTLP.Endpoint,
   384	                        ),
   385	                        telemetry.WithAttributes(
   386	                                semconv.ServiceNameKey.String(config.Trace.ServiceName),
   387	                                semconv.ServiceVersionKey.String(build.Version),
   388	                        ),
   389	                        telemetry.WithSamplingRatio(config.Trace.SampleRatio),
   390	                }
   391	
   392	                if !config.Trace.OTLP.TLS.Enabled {
   393	                        options = append(options, telemetry.WithOTLPInsecure())
   394	                }
   395	
   396	                tp := telemetry.MustNewTracerProvider(options...)
   397	                return func() error {
   398	                        // can take up to 5 seconds to complete (https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/aebcbfcbc2962957a578e9cb3e25dc834125e318/sdk/trace/batch_span_processor.go#L97)
   399	                        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 6*time.Second)
   400	                        defer cancel()
   401	                        return errors.Join(tp.ForceFlush(ctx), tp.Shutdown(ctx))
   402	                }
   403	        }
   404	        otel.SetTracerProvider(noop.NewTracerProvider())
   405	        return func() error {
   406	                return nil
   407	        }
   408	}

   410	func (s *ServerContext) datastoreConfig(config *serverconfig.Config) (storage.OpenFGADatastore, encoder.ContinuationTokenSerializer, error) {
   411	        // SQL Token Serializer by default
   412	        tokenSerializer := sqlcommon.NewSQLContinuationTokenSerializer()
   413	        datastoreOptions := []sqlcommon.DatastoreOption{
   414	                sqlcommon.WithSecondaryURI(config.Datastore.SecondaryURI),
   415	                sqlcommon.WithUsername(config.Datastore.Username),
   416	                sqlcommon.WithPassword(config.Datastore.Password),
   417	                sqlcommon.WithSecondaryUsername(config.Datastore.SecondaryUsername),
   418	                sqlcommon.WithSecondaryPassword(config.Datastore.SecondaryPassword),
   419	                sqlcommon.WithLogger(s.Logger),
   420	                sqlcommon.WithMaxTuplesPerWrite(config.MaxTuplesPerWrite),
   421	                sqlcommon.WithMaxTypesPerAuthorizationModel(config.MaxTypesPerAuthorizationModel),
   422	                sqlcommon.WithMaxOpenConns(config.Datastore.MaxOpenConns),
   423	                sqlcommon.WithMaxIdleConns(config.Datastore.MaxIdleConns),
   424	                sqlcommon.WithConnMaxIdleTime(config.Datastore.ConnMaxIdleTime),
   425	                sqlcommon.WithConnMaxLifetime(config.Datastore.ConnMaxLifetime),
   426	        }
   427	
   428	        if config.Datastore.Metrics.Enabled {
   429	                datastoreOptions = append(datastoreOptions, sqlcommon.WithMetrics())
   430	        }
   431	
   432	        dsCfg := sqlcommon.NewConfig(datastoreOptions...)
   433	
   434	        var datastore storage.OpenFGADatastore
   435	        var err error
   436	        switch config.Datastore.Engine {
   437	        case "memory":
   438	                // override for "memory" datastore
   439	                tokenSerializer = encoder.NewStringContinuationTokenSerializer()
   440	                opts := []memory.StorageOption{
   441	                        memory.WithMaxTypesPerAuthorizationModel(config.MaxTypesPerAuthorizationModel),
   442	                        memory.WithMaxTuplesPerWrite(config.MaxTuplesPerWrite),
   443	                }
   444	                datastore = memory.New(opts...)
   445	        case "mysql":
   446	                datastore, err = mysql.New(config.Datastore.URI, dsCfg)
   447	                if err != nil {
   448	                        return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize mysql datastore: %w", err)
   449	                }
   450	        case "postgres":
   451	                datastore, err = postgres.New(config.Datastore.URI, dsCfg)
   452	                if err != nil {
   453	                        return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize postgres datastore: %w", err)
   454	                }
   455	        case "sqlite":
   456	                datastore, err = sqlite.New(config.Datastore.URI, dsCfg)
   457	                if err != nil {
   458	                        return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize sqlite datastore: %w", err)
   459	                }
   460	        default:
   461	                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("storage engine '%s' is unsupported", config.Datastore.Engine)
   462	        }
   463	
   464	        s.Logger.Info(fmt.Sprintf("using '%v' storage engine", config.Datastore.Engine))
   465	
   466	        return datastore, tokenSerializer, nil
   467	}

   469	func (s *ServerContext) authenticatorConfig(config *serverconfig.Config) (authn.Authenticator, error) {
   470	        var authenticator authn.Authenticator
   471	        var err error
   472	
   473	        switch config.Authn.Method {
   474	        case "none":
   475	                s.Logger.Warn("authentication is disabled")
   476	                authenticator = authn.NoopAuthenticator{}
   477	        case "preshared":
   478	                s.Logger.Info("using 'preshared' authentication")
   479	                authenticator, err = presharedkey.NewPresharedKeyAuthenticator(config.Authn.Keys)
   480	        case "oidc":
   481	                s.Logger.Info("using 'oidc' authentication")
   482	                authenticator, err = oidc.NewRemoteOidcAuthenticator(config.Authn.Issuer, config.Authn.IssuerAliases, config.Authn.Audience, config.Authn.Subjects, config.Authn.ClientIDClaims)
   483	        default:
   484	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("unsupported authentication method '%v'", config.Authn.Method)
   485	        }
   486	        if err != nil {
   487	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize authenticator: %w", err)
   488	        }
   489	        return authenticator, nil
   490	}

        var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
        policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
        policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
        attempt := 1
        err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
                err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
                if err != nil {
                        cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
                        attempt++
                        return err
                }
                return nil
        }, policy)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
        }

        var collector prometheus.Collector
        if cfg.ExportMetrics {
                collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
                if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
                        return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
                }
        }

        stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
        dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

        return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}

// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
        primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
        }

        if secondaryDB != nil {
                secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
                }
        }
' --new_str 'func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
	attempt := 1
	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
		err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
		if err != nil {
			cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
			attempt++
			return err
		}
		return nil
	}, policy)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
	}

	var collector prometheus.Collector
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
		if err := prometheus.Register(prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}

// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
	}

	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
	if secondaryDB != nil {
		secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
		}
	}

   122	func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
   123	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
   124	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
   125	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
   126	attempt := 1
   127	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
   128	err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
   129	if err != nil {
   130	cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
   131	attempt++
   132	return err
   133	}
   134	return nil
   135	}, policy)
   136	if err != nil {
   137	return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
   138	}
   139	
   140	var collector prometheus.Collector
   141	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
   142	collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
   143	if err := prometheus.Register(prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)); err != nil {
   144	return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
   145	}
   146	}
   147	
   148	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
   149	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")
   150	
   151	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
   152	}
   153	
   154	// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
   155	func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
   156	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
   157	if err != nil {
   158	return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
   159	}
   160	
   161	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
   162	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
   163	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
   164	if secondaryDB != nil {
   165	secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
   166	if err != nil {
   167	return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
   168	}
   169	}

python3 -c '
import sys
path = "/testbed/pkg/storage/postgres/postgres.go"
with open(path, "r") as f:
    text = f.read()

# Fix the failed manual edits first if any
import re
# Restore to a clean state if possible, but I know what I did.
# I will just replace the whole functions.

configureDB_new = """func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
	attempt := 1
	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
		err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
		if err != nil {
			cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
			attempt++
			return err
		}
		return nil
	}, policy)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
	}

	var collector prometheus.Collector
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
		if name != "" {
			collector = prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)
		}
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}"""

NewWithDB_new = """func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
	}

	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
	if secondaryDB != nil {
		secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
		}
	}

	return &Datastore{
		primaryStbl:               primaryStbl,
		secondaryStbl:             secondaryStbl,
		primaryDB:                 primaryDB,
		secondaryDB:               secondaryDB,
		primaryDBInfo:             primaryDBInfo,
		secondaryDBInfo:           secondaryDBInfo,
		logger:                    cfg.Logger,
		primaryDBStatsCollector:   primaryCollector,
		secondaryDBStatsCollector: secondaryCollector,
		maxTuplesPerWriteField:    cfg.MaxTuplesPerWriteField,
		maxTypesPerModelField:     cfg.MaxTypesPerModelField,
		versionReady:              false,
	}, nil
}"""

# Use regex to find and replace the functions
text = re.sub(r"func configureDB\(.*?\n\}", configureDB_new, text, flags=re.DOTALL)
text = re.sub(r"func NewWithDB\(.*?\n\}", NewWithDB_new, text, flags=re.DOTALL)

with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(text)

configureDB_new = """func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
	attempt := 1
	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
		err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
		if err != nil {
			cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
			attempt++
			return err
		}
		return nil
	}, policy)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
	}

	var collector prometheus.Collector
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
		if name != "" {
			collector = prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)
		}
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}"""

		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
		if name != "" {
			collector = prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)
		}
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}"""

NewWithDB_new = """func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
	}

	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
	if secondaryDB != nil {
		secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
		}
	}

	return &Datastore{
		primaryStbl:               primaryStbl,
		secondaryStbl:             secondaryStbl,
		primaryDB:                 primaryDB,
		secondaryDB:               secondaryDB,
		primaryDBInfo:             primaryDBInfo,
		secondaryDBInfo:           secondaryDBInfo,
		logger:                    cfg.Logger,
		primaryDBStatsCollector:   primaryCollector,
		secondaryDBStatsCollector: secondaryCollector,
		maxTuplesPerWriteField:    cfg.MaxTuplesPerWriteField,
		maxTypesPerModelField:     cfg.MaxTypesPerModelField,
		versionReady:              false,
	}, nil
}"""

# Use regex to find and replace the functions
# Match configureDB up to its closing brace
text = re.sub(r"func configureDB\(.*?\n\}", configureDB_new, text, count=1, flags=re.DOTALL)
# Match NewWithDB up to its closing brace
text = re.sub(r"func NewWithDB\(.*?\n\}", NewWithDB_new, text, count=1, flags=re.DOTALL)

with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(text)

python3 -c '
import sys
import re
path = "/testbed/pkg/storage/postgres/postgres.go"
with open(path, "r") as f:
    text = f.read()

# Restore functions completely by finding the markers I know are there.
# We want to replace from the first "func configureDB" to the beginning of "func (s *Datastore) isSecondaryConfigured()"
match_start = text.find("func configureDB")
match_end = text.find("func (s *Datastore) isSecondaryConfigured()")

if match_start != -1 and match_end != -1:
    new_middle = """func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
	attempt := 1
	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
		err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
		if err != nil {
			cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
			attempt++
			return err
		}
		return nil
	}, policy)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
	}

	var collector prometheus.Collector
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
		if name != "" {
			collector = prometheus.WrapCollector(prometheus.Labels{"db": name}, collector)
		}
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}

// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
	}

	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
	if secondaryDB != nil {
		secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
		}
	}

	return &Datastore{
		primaryStbl:               primaryStbl,
		secondaryStbl:             secondaryStbl,
		primaryDB:                 primaryDB,
		secondaryDB:               secondaryDB,
		primaryDBInfo:             primaryDBInfo,
		secondaryDBInfo:           secondaryDBInfo,
		logger:                    cfg.Logger,
		primaryDBStatsCollector:   primaryCollector,
		secondaryDBStatsCollector: secondaryCollector,
		maxTuplesPerWriteField:    cfg.MaxTuplesPerWriteField,
		maxTypesPerModelField:     cfg.MaxTypesPerModelField,
		versionReady:              false,
	}, nil
}

"""
    text = text[:match_start] + new_middle + text[match_end:]

with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(text)
'

python3 -c "
import sys
import re
path = '/testbed/pkg/storage/postgres/postgres.go'
with open(path, 'r') as f:
    text = f.read()

# Replace Register with MustRegister or better, handle duplication by using Labels on collectors
# But wait, DBStatsCollector doesn'\''t take labels.
# Use a custom collector that wraps the sql.DBStats but adds labels.

new_collector_code = \"\"\"
type labeledStatsCollector struct {
	prometheus.Collector
	db    *sql.DB
	label string
}

func (l *labeledStatsCollector) Describe(ch chan<- *prometheus.Desc) {
	// We'\''ll compute the stats and describe them
}

func (l *labeledStatsCollector) Collect(ch chan<- prometheus.Metric) {
	stats := l.db.Stats()
	
	const namespace = \\\"openfga\\\"
	const subsystem = \\\"datastore\\\"
	
	ch <- prometheus.MustNewConstMetric(
		prometheus.NewDesc(
			prometheus.BuildFQName(namespace, subsystem, \\\"max_open_connections\\\"),
			\\\"Maximum number of open connections to the database.\\\",
			nil, prometheus.Labels{\\\"db\\\": l.label},
		),
		prometheus.GaugeValue,
		float64(stats.MaxOpenConnections),
	)
	// Add other metrics as needed... but wait, this is getting complicated.
}
\"\"\"
# Actually, prometheus.WrapCollector should be there if using a recent version. 
# Oh! I see what happened. I forgot to check the prometheus package documentation.
# For some reason my environment doesn'\''t have WrapCollector.

# Alternatives:
# 1. Use prometheus.NewRegistry() for each? No, we want them in the default registry.
# 2. Use labels.

# Let'\''s try to use a simpler approach to avoid duplicate registration.
# If it is the secondary DB, we just don'\''t register it for now? 
# No, the user wants metrics for both.

# Let'\''s look at what collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, \\\"openfga\\\") does.
# It uses the name as a prefix or namespace? 
# Usually it uses the string as a namespace. 

# If I change it to collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, \\\"openfga_secondary\\\") it will have different metric names!
# That would avoid the panic.

confirm_fix = \"\"\"
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		namespace := \\\"openfga\\\"
		if name != \\\"primary\\\" && name != \\\"\\\" {
			namespace = \\\"openfga_\\\" + name
		}
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, namespace)
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf(\\\"initialize metrics: %w\\\", err)
		}
	}
\"\"\"

# Wait, if I do this, both primary and secondary will have different namespaces.
# That'\''s a clean way to avoid registration conflict.

text = re.sub(r'if cfg\.ExportMetrics \{.*?if err := prometheus\.Register\(collector\); err != nil \{.*?\}', confirm_fix, text, count = 1, flags=re.DOTALL)
# It only replaced once because of count=1. Perfect. Oh wait, I need to do it correctly for the whole function.

with open(path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(text)
"

🎬 ACTION
python3 -c '
import sys
import re
path = "/testbed/pkg/storage/postgres/postgres.go"
with open(path, "r") as f:
    text = f.read()

# Restore functions completely by finding the markers I know are there.
# We want to replace from the first "func configureDB" to the beginning of "func (s *Datastore) isSecondaryConfigured()"
match_start = text.find("func configureDB")
match_end = text.find("func (s *Datastore) isSecondaryConfigured()")

if match_start != -1 and match_end != -1:
    new_middle = """func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
	attempt := 1
	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
		err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
		if err != nil {
			cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
			attempt++
			return err
		}
		return nil
	}, policy)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
	}

	var collector prometheus.Collector
	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
		namespace := "openfga"
		if name != "primary" && name != "" {
			namespace = "openfga_" + name
		}
		collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, namespace)
		if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
			return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
		}
	}

	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")

	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
}

// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
func NewWithDB(primaryDB, secondaryDB *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
	primaryDBInfo, primaryStbl, primaryCollector, err := configureDB(primaryDB, cfg, "primary")
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure primary db: %w", err)
	}

	var secondaryDBInfo *sqlcommon.DBInfo
	var secondaryStbl sq.StatementBuilderType
	var secondaryCollector prometheus.Collector
	if secondaryDB != nil {
		secondaryDBInfo, secondaryStbl, secondaryCollector, err = configureDB(secondaryDB, cfg, "secondary")
		if err != nil {
			return nil, fmt.Errorf("configure secondary db: %w", err)
		}
	}

	return &Datastore{
		primaryStbl:               primaryStbl,
		secondaryStbl:             secondaryStbl,
		primaryDB:                 primaryDB,
		secondaryDB:               secondaryDB,
		primaryDBInfo:             primaryDBInfo,
		secondaryDBInfo:           secondaryDBInfo,
		logger:                    cfg.Logger,
		primaryDBStatsCollector:   primaryCollector,
		secondaryDBStatsCollector: secondaryCollector,
		maxTuplesPerWriteField:    cfg.MaxTuplesPerWriteField,
		maxTypesPerModelField:     cfg.MaxTypesPerModelField,
		versionReady:              false,
	}, nil
}

"""
    text = text[:match_start] + new_middle + text[match_end:]

with open(path, "w") as f:
    f.write(text)
'

    77	// NewWithDB creates a new [Datastore] storage with the provided database connection.
    78	func NewWithDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config) (*Datastore, error) {
    79	        if cfg.MaxIdleConns != 0 {
    80	                db.SetMaxIdleConns(cfg.MaxIdleConns) // default is 2, not retaining connections(0) would be detrimental for performance
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        db.SetMaxOpenConns(cfg.MaxOpenConns)
    84	        db.SetConnMaxIdleTime(cfg.ConnMaxIdleTime)
    85	        db.SetConnMaxLifetime(cfg.ConnMaxLifetime)
    86	
    87	        policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
    88	        policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
    89	        attempt := 1
    90	        err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
    91	                err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
    92	                if err != nil {
    93	                        cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
    94	                        attempt++
    95	                        return err
    96	                }
    97	                return nil
    98	        }, policy)
    99	        if err != nil {
   100	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        var collector prometheus.Collector
   104	        if cfg.ExportMetrics {
   105	                collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, "openfga")
   106	                if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
   107	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
   108	                }
   109	        }
   110

   122	func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
   123	var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
   124	policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
   125	policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
   126	attempt := 1
   127	err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
   128	err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
   129	if err != nil {
   130	cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
   131	attempt++
   132	return err
   133	}
   134	return nil
   135	}, policy)
   136	if err != nil {
   137	return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
   138	}
   139	
   140	var collector prometheus.Collector
   141	if cfg.ExportMetrics {
   142	namespace := "openfga"
   143	if name != "primary" && name != "" {
   144	namespace = "openfga_" + name
   145	}
   146	collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, namespace)
   147	if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
   148	return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
   149	}
   150	}
   151	
   152	stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
   153	dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")
   154	
   155	return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
   156	}

+                                parsed.User = url.User(username)
+                        }
+                default:
+                        parsed.User = url.User(username)
+                }
+
+                uri = parsed.String()
+        }
+
+        db, err := sql.Open("pgx", uri)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize postgres connection: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        if cfg.MaxIdleConns != 0 {
+                db.SetMaxIdleConns(cfg.MaxIdleConns) // default is 2, not retaining connections(0) would be detrimental for performance
+        }
+
+        db.SetMaxOpenConns(cfg.MaxOpenConns)
+        db.SetConnMaxIdleTime(cfg.ConnMaxIdleTime)
+        db.SetConnMaxLifetime(cfg.ConnMaxLifetime)
+
+        return db, nil
 }

+func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
+var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
+policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
+policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
+attempt := 1
+err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
+err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
+if err != nil {
+cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
+attempt++
+return err
+}
+return nil
+}, policy)
+if err != nil {
+return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
+}
+
+var collector prometheus.Collector
+if cfg.ExportMetrics {
+namespace := "openfga"
+if name != "primary" && name != "" {
+namespace = "openfga_" + name
+}
+collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, namespace)
+if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
+return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
+}
+}
+
+stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
+dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")
+
+return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
 }

+        if consistency != nil && *consistency == openfgav1.ConsistencyPreference_HIGHER_CONSISTENCY {
+                // If we are using higher consistency, we need to use the write database.
+                return s.primaryStbl
+        }
+        if s.isSecondaryConfigured() {
+                // If we are using lower consistency, we can use the read database.
+                return s.secondaryStbl

+                        "relation":    filter.Relation,
+                        "_user":       targetUsersArg,
+                }).OrderBy("object_id")
+
+        if filter.ObjectIDs != nil && filter.ObjectIDs.Size() > 0 {
+                builder = builder.Where(sq.Eq{"object_id": filter.ObjectIDs.Values()})
+        }
+
+        return sqlcommon.NewSQLTupleIterator(builder, HandleSQLError), nil
 }

+        ctx, span := startTrace(ctx, "ReadAuthorizationModels")
+        defer span.End()
+
+        sb := s.getReadStbl(nil).
+                Select("authorization_model_id").
+                Distinct().
+                From("authorization_model").
+                Where(sq.Eq{"store": store}).
+                OrderBy("authorization_model_id desc")
+
+        if options.Pagination.From != "" {
+                sb = sb.Where(sq.LtOrEq{"authorization_model_id": options.Pagination.From})
+        }
+        if options.Pagination.PageSize > 0 {
+                sb = sb.Limit(uint64(options.Pagination.PageSize + 1)) // + 1 is used to determine whether to return a continuation token.
+        }
+
+        rows, err := sb.QueryContext(ctx)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+        defer rows.Close()
+
+        var modelIDs []string
+        var modelID string
+
+        for rows.Next() {
+                err = rows.Scan(&modelID)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+                }
+
+                modelIDs = append(modelIDs, modelID)
+        }
+
+        if err := rows.Err(); err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+
+        var token string
+        numModelIDs := len(modelIDs)
+        if len(modelIDs) > options.Pagination.PageSize {
+                numModelIDs = options.Pagination.PageSize
+                token = modelID
+        }
+
+        // TODO: make this concurrent with a maximum of 5 goroutines. This may be helpful:
+        // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/25306073/always-have-x-number-of-goroutines-running-at-any-time
+        models := make([]*openfgav1.AuthorizationModel, 0, numModelIDs)
+        // We use numModelIDs here to avoid retrieving possibly one extra model.
+        for i := 0; i < numModelIDs; i++ {
+                model, err := s.ReadAuthorizationModel(ctx, store, modelIDs[i])
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", err
+                }
+                models = append(models, model)
+        }
+
+        return models, token, nil
 }

+                if conditionName.String != "" {
+                        if conditionContext != nil {
+                                if err := proto.Unmarshal(conditionContext, &conditionContextStruct); err != nil {
+                                        return nil, "", err
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                tk := tupleUtils.NewTupleKeyWithCondition(
+                        tupleUtils.BuildObject(objectType, objectID),
+                        relation,
+                        user,
+                        conditionName.String,
+                        &conditionContextStruct,
+                )
+
+                changes = append(changes, &openfgav1.TupleChange{
+                        TupleKey:  tk,
+                        Operation: openfgav1.TupleOperation(operation),
+                        Timestamp: timestamppb.New(insertedAt.UTC()),
+                })
+        }
+
+        if len(changes) == 0 {
+                return nil, "", storage.ErrNotFound
+        }
+
+        return changes, ulid, nil
 }

+        ctx, span := startTrace(ctx, "ReadAuthorizationModels")
+        defer span.End()
+
+        sb := s.getReadStbl(nil).
+                Select("authorization_model_id").
+                Distinct().
+                From("authorization_model").
+                Where(sq.Eq{"store": store}).
+                OrderBy("authorization_model_id desc")
+
+        if options.Pagination.From != "" {
+                sb = sb.Where(sq.LtOrEq{"authorization_model_id": options.Pagination.From})
+        }
+        if options.Pagination.PageSize > 0 {
+                sb = sb.Limit(uint64(options.Pagination.PageSize + 1)) // + 1 is used to determine whether to return a continuation token.
+        }
+
+        rows, err := sb.QueryContext(ctx)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+        defer rows.Close()
+
+        var modelIDs []string
+        var modelID string
+
+        for rows.Next() {
+                err = rows.Scan(&modelID)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+                }
+
+                modelIDs = append(modelIDs, modelID)
+        }
+
+        if err := rows.Err(); err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+
+        var token string
+        numModelIDs := len(modelIDs)
+        if len(modelIDs) > options.Pagination.PageSize {
+                numModelIDs = options.Pagination.PageSize
+                token = modelID
+        }
+
+        // TODO: make this concurrent with a maximum of 5 goroutines. This may be helpful:
+        // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/25306073/always-have-x-number-of-goroutines-running-at-any-time
+        models := make([]*openfgav1.AuthorizationModel, 0, numModelIDs)
+        // We use numModelIDs here to avoid retrieving possibly one extra model.
+        for i := 0; i < numModelIDs; i++ {
+                model, err := s.ReadAuthorizationModel(ctx, store, modelIDs[i])
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", err
+                }
+                models = append(models, model)
+        }
+
+        return models, token, nil
 }

+                        Timestamp: timestamppb.New(insertedAt.UTC()),
+                })
+        }
+

+                return nil, "", storage.ErrNotFound
+        }

+func configureDB(db *sql.DB, cfg *sqlcommon.Config, name string) (*sqlcommon.DBInfo, sq.StatementBuilderType, prometheus.Collector, error) {
+var stbl sq.StatementBuilderType
+policy := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()
+policy.MaxElapsedTime = 1 * time.Minute
+attempt := 1
+err := backoff.Retry(func() error {
+err := db.PingContext(context.Background())
+if err != nil {
+cfg.Logger.Info("waiting for database", zap.Int("attempt", attempt))
+attempt++
+return err
+}
+return nil
+}, policy)
+if err != nil {
+return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("ping db: %w", err)
+}
+
+var collector prometheus.Collector
+if cfg.ExportMetrics {
+namespace := "openfga"
+if name != "primary" && name != "" {
+namespace = "openfga_" + name
+}
+collector = collectors.NewDBStatsCollector(db, namespace)
+if err := prometheus.Register(collector); err != nil {
+return nil, stbl, nil, fmt.Errorf("initialize metrics: %w", err)
+}
+}
+
+stbl = sq.StatementBuilder.PlaceholderFormat(sq.Dollar).RunWith(db)
+dbInfo := sqlcommon.NewDBInfo(db, stbl, HandleSQLError, "postgres")
+
+return dbInfo, stbl, collector, nil
 }

+                return s.primaryStbl

+                From("authorization_model").
+                Where(sq.Eq{"store": store}).
+                OrderBy("authorization_model_id desc")
+
+        if options.Pagination.From != "" {
+                sb = sb.Where(sq.LtOrEq{"authorization_model_id": options.Pagination.From})
+        }
+        if options.Pagination.PageSize > 0 {
+                sb = sb.Limit(uint64(options.Pagination.PageSize + 1)) // + 1 is used to determine whether to return a continuation token.
+        }
+
+        rows, err := sb.QueryContext(ctx)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+        defer rows.Close()
+
+        var modelIDs []string
+        var modelID string
+
+        for rows.Next() {
+                err = rows.Scan(&modelID)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+                }
+
+                modelIDs = append(modelIDs, modelID)
+        }
+
+        if err := rows.Err(); err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+
+        var token string
+        numModelIDs := len(modelIDs)
+        if len(modelIDs) > options.Pagination.PageSize {
+                numModelIDs = options.Pagination.PageSize
+                token = modelID
+        }
+
+        // TODO: make this concurrent with a maximum of 5 goroutines. This may be helpful:
+        // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/25306073/always-have-x-number-of-goroutines-running-at-any-time
+        models := make([]*openfgav1.AuthorizationModel, 0, numModelIDs)
+        // We use numModelIDs here to avoid retrieving possibly one extra model.
+        for i := 0; i < numModelIDs; i++ {
+                model, err := s.ReadAuthorizationModel(ctx, store, modelIDs[i])
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", err
+                }
+                models = append(models, model)
+        }
+
+        return models, token, nil
 }

+        ctx, span := startTrace(ctx, "ReadChanges")
+        defer span.End()
+
+        objectTypeFilter := filter.ObjectType
+        horizonOffset := filter.HorizonOffset
+
+        orderBy := "ulid asc"
+        if options.SortDesc {
+                orderBy = "ulid desc"
+        }
+
+        sb := s.getReadStbl(nil).
+                Select(
+                        "ulid", "object_type", "object_id", "relation",
+                        "_user",
+                        "operation",
+                        "condition_name", "condition_context", "inserted_at",
+                ).
+                From("changelog").
+                Where(sq.Eq{"store": store}).
+                Where(fmt.Sprintf("inserted_at < NOW() - interval '%dms'", horizonOffset.Milliseconds())).
+                OrderBy(orderBy)
+
+        if objectTypeFilter != "" {
+                sb = sb.Where(sq.Eq{"object_type": objectTypeFilter})
+        }
+        if options.Pagination.From != "" {
+                sb = sqlcommon.AddFromUlid(sb, options.Pagination.From, options.SortDesc)
+        }
+        if options.Pagination.PageSize > 0 {
+                sb = sb.Limit(uint64(options.Pagination.PageSize)) // + 1 is NOT used here as we always return a continuation token.
+        }
+
+        rows, err := sb.QueryContext(ctx)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+        }
+        defer rows.Close()
+
+        var changes []*openfgav1.TupleChange
+        var ulid string
+        for rows.Next() {
+                var objectType, objectID, relation, user string
+                var operation int
+                var insertedAt time.Time
+                var conditionName sql.NullString
+                var conditionContext []byte
+
+                err = rows.Scan(
+                        &ulid,
+                        &objectType,
+                        &objectID,
+                        &relation,
+                        &user,
+                        &operation,
+                        &conditionName,
+                        &conditionContext,
+                        &insertedAt,
+                )
+                if err != nil {
+                        return nil, "", HandleSQLError(err)
+                }
+
+                var conditionContextStruct structpb.Struct
+                if conditionName.String != "" {
+                        if conditionContext != nil {
+                                if err := proto.Unmarshal(conditionContext, &conditionContextStruct); err != nil {
+                                        return nil, "", err
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                tk := tupleUtils.NewTupleKeyWithCondition(
+                        tupleUtils.BuildObject(objectType, objectID),
+                        relation,
+                        user,
+                        conditionName.String,
+                        &conditionContextStruct,
+                )
+
+                changes = append(changes, &openfgav1.TupleChange{
+                        TupleKey:  tk,
+                        Operation: openfgav1.TupleOperation(operation),
+                        Timestamp: timestamppb.New(insertedAt.UTC()),
+                })
+        }
+
+        if len(changes) == 0 {
+                return nil, "", storage.ErrNotFound
+        }
+
+        return changes, ulid, nil
 }
